          Since we understand technology from both a hardware and software perspective, we are able to provide technology support services unmatched by software-only or hardware-only providers. We also complement our expertise with a strong set of technology partners.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="col-md-4 col-xs-12">
        <div class="about-item">
         <span class="fa fa-lightbulb-o">
         </span>
         <h4>
          Tailored Solutions
         </h4>
         <p>
          Have an idea but can't get the technology pieces to "fit"? The pace of change in the industry during the last couple of years is breath-taking, so we understand that keeping up to date is a challenge. We'll help you to sort through technology options so you can achieve your vision.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <!--//row-->
     </div>
     <!--//container-->
    </section>
    <!-- SECTION : TECHNOLOGIES -->
    <section class="technologies section has-bg-color padded-section" id="technologies">
     <div class="container">
      <h1 class="title text-center">
       Cutting Edge Technologies
      </h1>
      <p class="intro text-center">
       Whether your business is in the mobile, training, simulation, wireless tracking, mapping, healthcare, or other technology-intensive space we have the software and hardware capabilities to develop and integrate end-to-end solutions. Abamis engineers have experience in electronics and embedded hardware development, which provides a balanced approach in situations where software and hardware must work well together.
       <br/>
       <br/>
       Take a look at the technology areas we have expertise in, and then explore our portfolio for relevant use cases and in-depth analysis of specific application solutions.
      </p>
      <div id="technologies-carousel-container">
       <div id="technologies-carousel">
        <!-- Technologies Section Content -->
        <div class="technology">
         <span class="tech-icon ti-1">
          <span class="fa fa-apple">
          </span>
         </span>
         <h4>
          Mobile and Social
         </h4>
         <p>
          We build apps for Apple iOS, Android, and Windows using programming languages such as Objective-C, Swift, Java, JavaScript, and C#, or through higher level platforms such as Appcelerator Titanium and Unity. Our backend cloud solutions give you access to manage, control, message, and report on advertising and usage statistics. We also develop software for wireless devices including Bluetooth Smart tags, wearable sensors, and smartwatches such as the Apple Watch.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="technology">
         <span class="tech-icon ti-2">
          <span class="fa fa-cloud">
          </span>
         </span>
         <h4>
          Cloud Computing
         </h4>
         <p>
          A reliable cloud-based solution requires experience not just in a particular cloud platform, but also in understanding the integration requirements that connect all the platform elements together. Custom solutions can range from shared hosting, to VPS, to cloud-based solutions using Amazon AWS, Google Cloud, or Microsoft Azure. For solutions that need backend databases, social interaction, analytics, and reporting our experience includes Google Analytics, Parse, and Flurry.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="technology">
         <span class="tech-icon ti-3">
          <span class="fa fa-gamepad">
          </span>
         </span>
         <h4>
          3D Gaming and Simulation
         </h4>
         <p>
          An engaging 3D game or experience keeps users coming back for more. Our solutions include the development of first-person games, training simulations, and avatar-based virtual reality experiences for caregiver education. Technologies we are acquainted with include Unity 3D, OpenGL, Direct3D, and high-level interfaces for providing animations, special effects, custom shaders and rendering, user interface elements, physics modeling, and augmented-reality applications.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="technology">
         <span class="tech-icon ti-4">
          <span class="fa fa-html5">
          </span>
         </span>
         <h4>
          Web Design
         </h4>
         <p>
          Your web site needs to be accessible from a variety of devices and be responsive to changes in form factor and user interfaces. It must also be visually appealing but also fast to load and efficient in less powerful devices. We use and work with a variety of web technologies including Apache, ASP.NET, Bootstrap, Django, Drupal, eCommerce platforms, Google Maps, JavaScript, MySQL, Node.js, Python, and Ruby.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="technology">
         <span class="tech-icon ti-5">
          <span class="fa fa-video-camera">
          </span>
         </span>
         <h4>
          Video and Image Processing
         </h4>
         <p>
          From video streaming to real-time stereo 3D recovery to facial recognition systems, Abamis provides solutions for addressing some of the most challenging video and image processing problems. We have used OpenCV, OpenCL, CUDA, and other GPU-based approaches to address high-performance computation and cross-platform solutions. We have also developed extensions and plugins for products such as Unity 3D, Maya, and NUKE.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="technology">
         <span class="tech-icon ti-6">
          <span class="fa fa-bluetooth-b">
          </span>
         </span>
         <h4>
          Wireless
         </h4>
         <p>
          The Internet of Things (IoT) is revolutionizing the way we interact with our environment, gather real-time sensor data, and trigger actions and activities. We have developed radio-based applications to support systems for remote sensor data gathering, wearables, asset tracking, manufacturing, home automation, and robotics. We communicate with cloud backends using Bluetooth Smart (BLE), WiFi, GSM/3G/LTE, or custom RF protocols.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="technology">
         <span class="tech-icon ti-7">
          <span class="fa fa-microchip">
          </span>
         </span>
         <h4>
          Embedded Solutions
         </h4>
         <p>
          Whether you want to build your prototype using Arduino, BeagleBone, or a Raspberry Pi we have the expertise to get your embedded projects to a demo-ready state. Our in-house expertise and our technology partners can take your ideas from concept to schematic, PCB, assembly, case design, software development, and product ready with quick turn-around and cost-effective approaches.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="technology">
         <span class="tech-icon ti-8">
          <span class="fa fa-server">
          </span>
         </span>
         <h4>
          AI and High Performance Computing
         </h4>
         <p>
          Artificial Intelligence applications are generally computationally demanding, requiring expertise in parallel computing environments and libraries such as OpenCL and CUDA. Our engineers develop IoT and Big Data applications using machine learning and AI algorithms for real-time predictive analytics, data mining, and visualization.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="technology">
         <span class="tech-icon ti-9">
          <span class="fa fa-users">
          </span>
         </span>
         <h4>
          STEM and Outreach
         </h4>
         <p>
          We support STEM-related activities by making presentations on technology, participating in local robotics and electronics clubs, and performing technology demonstrations at the Orlando Science Center, The Dorothy Lumley Melrose Center, and the Maker Faire activities and Meetups happening in the area. We also love teaching coding at the popular
          <a href="https://hourofcode.com">
           Hour of Code
          </a>
          .
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
       <a class="left carousel-control" id="technologies-carousel-prev">
        <span class="fa fa-chevron-left fa-4">
         <span class="sr-only">
          Cycle list of technologies left.
         </span>
        </span>
       </a>
       <a class="right carousel-control" id="technologies-carousel-next">
        <span class="fa fa-chevron-right fa-4">
         <span class="sr-only">
          Cycle list of technologies right.
         </span>
        </span>
       </a>
      </div>
     </div>
    </section>
